* Idea
The idea is to create a "replica" of the PCAD in [[https://simgrid.org/doc/latest/index.html][SimGrid]] using the C++ interface

* Code
** Makefile
#+begin_src makefile :tangle Makefile
CPPC=g++
CPPFLAGS=-shared -Wall -Werror -fPIC
LIBS=simgrid

.PHONY: clean platform

export PKG_CONFIG_PATH := /opt/simgrid/lib/pkgconfig:$(PKG_CONFIG_PATH) # export installation path to simgrid

pcad:
	g++ -shared -fPIC -o pcad.so create-pcad.cpp `pkg-config --cflags --libs $(LIBS)`

base:
	g++ -shared -fPIC -o libgriffon_platform.so base.cpp `pkg-config --cflags --libs $(LIBS)`

clean:
	rm -f *.so
#+end_src

** e example (from simgrid docs)
#+begin_src C++ :tangle base.cpp :results output :exports both :main no
/* Copyright (c) 2006-2025. The SimGrid Team. All rights reserved.          */

/* This program is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify it
 * under the terms of the license (GNU LGPL) which comes with this package. */

#include <numeric>
#include <simgrid/s4u.hpp>
namespace sg4 = simgrid::s4u;

/**
 * @brief Create a new cabinet
 *
 * This function creates the cabinet, adding the hosts and links properly.
 * See figure below for more details of each cabinet
 *
 * @param root Root netzone
 * @param name Cabinet name
 * @param radicals IDs of nodes inside the cabinet
 * @return netzone the created netzone
 */
static sg4::NetZone* create_cabinet(sg4::NetZone* root, const std::string& name, const std::vector<int>& radicals)
{
  auto* cluster      = root->add_netzone_star(name);
  std::string prefix = "griffon-";
  std::string suffix = ".nancy.grid5000.fr";

  /* create the backbone link */
  const sg4::Link* l_bb = cluster->add_link("backbone-" + name, "1.25GBps");
  sg4::LinkInRoute backbone(l_bb);

  /* create all hosts and connect them to outside world */
  for (const auto& id : radicals) {
    std::string hostname = prefix + std::to_string(id) + suffix;
    /* create host */
    const sg4::Host* host = cluster->add_host(hostname, "286.087kf");
    /* create UP/DOWN link */
    const sg4::Link* link = cluster->add_split_duplex_link(hostname, "125MBps")->set_latency("24us");

    /* add link and backbone for communications from the host */
    cluster->add_route(host, nullptr, {{link, sg4::LinkInRoute::Direction::UP}, backbone}, true);
  }

  /* create gateway */

  cluster->set_gateway(cluster->add_router(prefix + name + "-router" + suffix));

  cluster->seal();
  return cluster;
}

/** @brief Programmatic version of griffon.xml */
extern "C" void load_platform(sg4::Engine& e);
void load_platform(sg4::Engine& e)
{
  /**
   * C++ version of griffon.xml
   * Old Grid5000 cluster (not available anymore): 3 cabinets containing homogeneous nodes connected through a backbone
   *                                  1.25GBps shared link
   *                          ___________________________________
   *          1              /                |                  \
   *                        /                 |                   \
   *                       /                  |                    \
   *     ________________ /             ______|__________           \_________________
   *     |               |              |               |            |               |
   *     | cab1 router   |              | cab2 router   |            | cab3 router   |
   *     |_______________|              |_______________|            |_______________|
   *     ++++++++++++++++               ++++++++++++++++             ++++++++++++++++++  <-- 1.25 backbone
   *     / /   | |    \ \              / /    | |    \ \             / /     | |     \ \
   *    / /    | |     \ \            / /     | |     \ \           / /      | |      \ \ <-- 125Mbps links
   *   / /     | |      \ \          / /      | |      \ \         / /       | |       \ \
   * host1     ...      hostN      host1      ...      hostM      host1      ...       hostQ
   */

  auto* root = e.get_netzone_root()->add_netzone_star("AS_griffon");

  /* create top link */
  const sg4::Link* l_bb = root->add_link("backbone", "1.25GBps")->set_latency("24us")->seal();
  sg4::LinkInRoute backbone{l_bb};

  /* create cabinet1 */
  std::vector<int> rad(32);
  std::iota(rad.begin(), rad.end(), 1); // 1-29,58,59,60
  rad[rad.size() - 1]  = 60;
  rad[rad.size() - 2]  = 59;
  rad[rad.size() - 3]  = 58;
  const sg4::NetZone* cab_zone = create_cabinet(root, "cabinet1", rad);
  root->add_route(cab_zone, nullptr, {backbone});

  /* create cabinet2 */
  rad.resize(28);
  std::iota(rad.begin(), rad.end(), 30); // 30-57
  cab_zone = create_cabinet(root, "cabinet2", rad);
  root->add_route(cab_zone, nullptr, {backbone});

  /* create cabinet3 */
  rad.resize(32);
  std::iota(rad.begin(), rad.end(), 61); // 61-92
  cab_zone = create_cabinet(root, "cabinet3", rad);
  root->add_route(cab_zone, nullptr, {backbone});

  root->seal();
}
#+end_src

** Create PCAD

This currently has rack2 with cei and draco and rack4 with tupi and poti (not
fully configurated). Based on the simgrid example.

*** Libraries and namespace
#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both
#include <numeric>
#include <simgrid/s4u.hpp>
#include <fstream>

namespace sg4 = simgrid::s4u;
#+end_src

*** Structs
#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both
typedef struct partition {
  std::string name;
  std::string calib_file;
  std::string speed;
  std::string bw;
  std::string lat;
  std::string switch_ref;
  int count;
  int cores; // Only counting phisical cores
} partition_t;

typedef struct switch_info {
  std::string name;
  std::string capacity;
  std::string latency;
} switch_t;

#+end_src

*** Helper function to load calibration

#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both
std::map<std::string, std::string> load_calibration(const std::string& filename) {
  std::map<std::string, std::string> props;
  if (filename.empty()) return props; // Retorna vazio se não houver arquivo

  std::ifstream file(filename);
  std::string line;

  while (std::getline(file, line)) {
    auto delim = line.find('=');
    if (delim != std::string::npos) {
      std::string key = line.substr(0, delim);
      std::string value = line.substr(delim + 1);
      props[key] = value;
    }
  }
  return props;
}
#+end_src
*** Generic function to create one partition
#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both

/*
 @brief Create a partition with N machines

 This function creates the any partition, adding the hosts and links properly.
 @param root Root netzone
 @param switch_fatpipe Switch link for the rack to model the connection
 @param partition Information about the hosts in the partition
,*/

void create_partition(sg4::NetZone* rack,
                      sg4::Link* switch_cable,
		      partition_t partition)
{

  auto calib_props = load_calibration(partition.calib_file);

  for (int id = 1; id <= partition.count; id++) {
    std::string hostname = partition.name + std::to_string(id);

    auto* host = rack->add_host(hostname, partition.speed)->set_core_count(partition.cores);

    for (const auto& [key, value] : calib_props) {
        host->set_property(key, value);
    }

    host->seal();

    auto* node_cable = rack->add_link(hostname + "_cable", partition.bw)->set_latency(partition.lat)->seal();

    // Looks like StarZone automatically calculates the path to the netzone gateway when the second argument is a nullptr
    rack->add_route(host,
                    nullptr,
                    std::vector<const sg4::Link*>{node_cable, switch_cable});
  }
}

#+end_src
*** Generic function to create one rack
#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both
/**
 ,* @brief Create a rack with N partitions
 ,*
 ,* This function creates the a rack, adding the internal partitions linked correctly.
 ,*
 ,* @param root Root netzone
 ,* @param rack_name Rack name
 ,* @param partitions Vector with the partitions information
 ,*/
sg4::NetZone *create_rack(sg4::NetZone *root, std::string rack_name,
			  std::vector<switch_t> switches,
                          std::vector<partition_t> partitions)
    {

      auto* rack_zone = root->add_netzone_star(rack_name);
      auto* rack_router = rack_zone->add_router(rack_name + "_router");
      rack_zone->set_gateway(rack_router); // rack gateaway


      std::map<std::string, sg4::Link*> switch_links;

      for(const auto& sw : switches) {
	auto* cable = rack_zone->add_link(rack_name + "_" + sw.name, sw.capacity)
	  ->set_latency(sw.latency)
	  ->set_sharing_policy(sg4::Link::SharingPolicy::FATPIPE)
	  ->seal();

	switch_links[sw.name] = cable;
      }

      // // Create Fatpipe to simulat the switch
      // auto* rack_switch_fatpipe = rack_zone->add_link(rack_name + "_fatpipe", switch_capacity)
      // 	->set_latency(switch_latency)
      // 	->set_sharing_policy(sg4::Link::SharingPolicy::SHARED)
      // 	->seal();

      // Nodes partitions (nodes)
      for(const auto& partition : partitions){
	create_partition(rack_zone, switch_links[partition.switch_ref], partition);

      }

      rack_zone->seal();
      return rack_zone;
}
#+end_src

#+begin_src C++ :results output :exports both

/** @brief Programmatic version of PCAD */
extern "C" void load_platform(sg4::Engine& e);
void load_platform(sg4::Engine& e)
{
  auto* root = e.get_netzone_root();

  switch_t r2_sw_10gb = {"switch_10gb", "10Gbps", "100ns"};
  switch_t r2_sw_1gb  = {"switch_1gb", "1Gbps", "100ns"};
  std::vector<switch_t> rack2_switches = {r2_sw_10gb, r2_sw_1gb};

  // partition_t cei = {"cei", "", "19.125Gf", "9.413Gbps", "124us", 6, 24};
  partition_t cei = {"cei", "cei.txt", "19.125Gf", "10Gbps", "124us", "switch_10gb", 6, 24};
  // partition_t draco = {"draco", "draco.txt", "14.125Gf", "941Mbps", "115us", 6, 16};
  partition_t draco = {"draco", "draco.txt", "14.125Gf", "1Gbps", "115us", "switch_1gb", 6, 16};
  std::vector<partition_t> rack2_partitions = {cei, draco};

  sg4::NetZone *rack2_zone = create_rack(root, "rack2", rack2_switches, rack2_partitions);

  // =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= RACK 4 =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=

  switch_t r4_sw_1gb = {"switch_1gb", "1Gbps", "100ns"};
  std::vector<switch_t> rack4_switches = {r4_sw_1gb};

  partition_t poti = {"poti", "", "20.2Gf", "940Mbps", "117us", "switch_1gb", 5, 20};
  // partition_t tupi = {"tupi", "tupi.txt", "58.375Gf", "942Mbps", "87us", 6, 8};
  partition_t tupi = {"tupi", "tupi.txt", "58.375Gf", "1Gbps", "87us", "switch_1gb", 6, 8};
  std::vector<partition_t> rack4_partitions = {poti, tupi};

  sg4::NetZone *rack4_zone = create_rack(root, "rack4", rack4_switches, rack4_partitions);

  // =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= CONNECTION BETWEEN THE RACKS (switchs) =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=
  std::string inter_switch_bw = "10Gbps";
  std::string inter_switch_lat = "50us";

  auto* link_rack2_gw = root->add_link("link_rack2_gateway", inter_switch_bw)->set_latency(inter_switch_lat)->seal();
  auto* link_rack4_gw = root->add_link("link_rack4_gateway", inter_switch_bw)->set_latency(inter_switch_lat)->seal();

  // auto* rack_link = root->add_link("r2_to_r4_cable", inter_switch_bw)
  //   ->set_latency(inter_switch_lat)
  //   ->seal();

  root->add_route(rack2_zone, rack4_zone, std::vector<const sg4::Link*>{link_rack2_gw, link_rack4_gw});
  // connect the zones
  // root->add_route(rack2_zone, rack4_zone, {rack_link});

  root->seal();
}
#+end_src

enable a scalatable creation using vectors. Each position is a
partition configuration (name, speed, bw and lat) of the host.


[17:19:15; 22.12.2025]: Created a script using the "amigo" to verify
the topology: =verify-platform.cpp=. The section about latency is not
important by now since it is hardcoded with the random value, but the
connections are

Compile the program:
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
g++ verify-platform.cpp create-pcad.cpp -o verify_platform `pkg-config --cflags --libs simgrid`
#+end_src

Convert topology.dot to png.
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
dot -Tpng topology.dot -o topology.png
#+end_src

** 2025-12-24: More generic and abstract creation of platform

[14:11:07; 24.12.2025]: I make it easier to create a rack by using a
partition struct and a create_rack function. As we are modeling just
two racks, and don't need to automatically link the racks, but if the
number of racks grows, it is possible to create and link the racks
automatically using two nested FORs.

[20:16:34; 26.01.2026]: Today was a busy (and a little disappointing)

[20:41:45; 26.01.2026]: HPL has a hpl.dat file that configures the
execution. Correctly configuring it looks essential for a honest
result.
https://netlib.org/benchmark/hpl/tuning.html
https://www.netlib.org/benchmark/hpl/faqs.html

N: 80 % of the total amount of memory is a good guess
Nb: The bottom line is that "good" block sizes are almost always in the [32 .. 256] interval.


[21:17:45; 26.01.2026]: I will use guix while pcad don't have nix at
the moment.

Save the channels from the experiment time
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
guix describe -f channels > channels.scm
#+end_src

Using channel and manifest to full reproducibility
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
guix time-machine -C channels.scm -- shell -m manifest.scm
#+end_src

Using the shell (=--pure= removes everything else):
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
guix shell --pure -m manifest.scm
#+end_src


Manifesto para o hpl:
#+begin_src shell :tangle manifest.scm :results output :exports both
(specifications->manifest
  '("hpl"
    "openmpi"
    "coreutils")) ; Adiciona ls, cp, cat, etc.
#+end_src


Code to get NB:
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
echo "scale=0; 0.8*sqrt($(free -b | awk '{print $3}' | sed "2q;d")/8) / 1" | bc
#+end_src

Last division by one is from here:
https://askubuntu.com/questions/217570/bc-set-number-of-digits-after-decimal-point

***** Grouping
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df |> group_by(Machine, NB) |>
  summarize(
    n = n(),
    sd = sd(GFlops),
    se = (3 * sd) / sqrt(n),
    sd_time = sd(Time), # [19:49:40; 04.02.2026]: Even the time is variating a lot, maybe I need to control better
    time = sum(Time)/60,
    GF = mean(GFlops)
  )

#+end_src

#+begin_src python :results output :exports both
import itertools
import random

random.seed(0) # [20:54:22; 05.02.2026]: I added the seed here, I think it is better to be
               #                         deterministic for the good of reproductibility :)

op = ['Recv', 'Isend', 'PingPong', 'Wtime', 'Wtime', 'Iprobe', 'Test']
sizes = [int(10**random.uniform(0, 9)) for _ in range(100)]
exp = list(itertools.product(op, sizes))
exp *= 50
random.shuffle(exp)

# print('operation, size') [20:55:17; 05.02.2026]: Also removed the header
for op, size in exp:
    print('%s, %d' % (op, size))
#+end_src

[20:56:33; 05.02.2026]: I will probably need to nodes two nodes for
the calibration. I will create a slurm for the calibration and let it
run today.


#+begin_src shell :tangle slurm/mpi-calibration.slurm :results output :exports both
#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name=Network_Calibration_SIMGRID
#partition will be defined by the command line call of sbatch
#SBATCH --nodes=2
#SBATCH --time=24:00:00
#SBATCH --output=%N_%x_%j.out
#SBATCH --error=%N_%x_%j.err

date +%D-%T 2>&1

set -euo pipefail

MACHINEFILE="nodes.$SLURM_JOB_ID"
srun -l hostname | sort -n | awk '{print $2}' > $MACHINEFILE

HOST_IDS=$(paste -sd '-' $MACHINEFILE)

DIR="calibration-$HOST_IDS-`date +%d-%m-%s`-$SLURM_JOB_ID"
mkdir $DIR

EXP_FILE="${DIR}/exp_sizes_${SLURM_JOB_ID}.csv"

make
python3 generate_size_file.py > $EXP_FILE

mpirun -np 2 -machinefile $MACHINEFILE ./calibrate -d $DIR -m 0 -M 1000000000 -p "exp-$SLURM_JOB_ID" -s $EXP_FILE

date +%D-%T 2>&1
#+end_src

#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name=calibracao_simgrid
#SBATCH --nodes=2
#SBATCH --ntasks-per-node=1
#SBATCH --time=00:10:00
#SBATCH --output=calibracao_%j.out
#SBATCH --error=calibracao_%j.err

nodes=$(scontrol show hostnames $SLURM_JOB_NODELIST)
nodes_array=($nodes)

server=${nodes_array[0]}
client=${nodes_array[1]}

echo "Server: $server"
echo "Client: $client"
echo "Starting server at $server"
srun --nodes=1 --nodelist=$server guix shell iperf -- iperf3 -s &
SERVER_PID=$!

sleep 1

# Doing 3 executions of 10 seconds (is this in any possible way better then a execution of 30 seconds?)

for i in 1 2 3; do
    echo "Run $i at $client"
    srun --nodes=1 --nodelist=$client guix shell iperf -- iperf3 -c $server -t 10 -O 3 --no-delay
done

kill $SERVER_PID
#+end_src

#+begin_src shell :tangle data/mpi-calibration/create_zip.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :results output :exports both
for i in `find exps/ -type d`; do
    exp=$i
    if [[ -n `echo $exp | grep -- "-12-"` ]]; then
	     echo $exp
	     partition=$(echo $exp | cut -d- -f2 | sed "s/[0-9]*//g")
	     for f in $exp/*; do
		      exp_file=$(echo $f | rev | cut -d/ -f 1 | rev | sed "s/-[0-9]*//g")
		      cp $f ./$exp_file
	     done

	     cp `echo $partition | tr -d '\r' | xargs`?.out breakpoints

	     zip $partition.zip breakpoints exp_*
	     rm breakpoints exp_*
    fi;
done

#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
load <- function(dir=".", regex="s\\/results.csv") {

  options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
  suppressMessages(library(fs))
  suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

  BASE <- dir
  tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = regex, recurse=TRUE)) |> print() |>
    mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
    unnest(DATA)
}

df.machine <- load("data/hpl/", ".csv$") |>
  group_by(machine, n, nb, p, q) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_gflops=mean(gflops),
    sd_g = sd(gflops),
    se_g = (3 * sd_g) / sqrt(N),
  ) |> print(n=100)
#+end_src

**** Bandwidth
For the bandwidth based on the iperf3:

#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both :tangle data/iperf3/create_csv.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755)
echo "client,server,mean_speed_mega"

for f in *calibracao*; do
    SER=$(cat $f | grep Server: | cut -d: -f2 | xargs)

    CLI=$(cat $f | grep Client: | cut -d: -f2 | xargs)

    cat $f | grep sender | \
    sed -E "s/.* ([0-9.]+ .)bits.*/\1/g" | \
    sed "s/ M//g" | sed "s/ G/\*1000/g" |\
    bc -l | sed "s/^/$CLI,$SER,/g"
done

#+end_src

[20:13:19; 21.02.2026]: The iperf experiment was consisted of 3
executions of 10 seconds comm between two machines in the
cluster. This experiment was execute twice. In total we have 60
samples per partition

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
load <- function(dir=".", regex=".csv$") {

  options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
  suppressMessages(library(fs))
  suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

  BASE <- dir
  tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = regex, recurse=TRUE)) |> print() |>
    mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
    unnest(DATA) |> select(-CSV)
}

df <- load("data/iperf3/", ".csv$") |>
  mutate(partition = gsub("[0-9]*", "", client)) |>
  group_by(partition)

df |> print(n=100) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_comm=mean(mean_speed_mega),
    sd_c = sd(mean_speed_mega),
    se_c = (3 * sd_c) / sqrt(N),
    cv = sd_c/mean_comm
  )

#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
#+begin_example
# A tibble: 1 × 1
  CSV
  <fs::path>
1 data/iperf3/iperf-results.csv
# A tibble: 24 × 4

**** Latency with ping

[20:29:41; 21.02.2026]: To measure the latency with ping I will use
half of the mean time for the ping command (ping gets the time to go
and come back)

[20:32:18; 21.02.2026]: I will run again because i used the quiet mode
so I can't measure the variancy...

[23:04:29; 21.02.2026]: The ping experience was made by running for
executions of ping between to machines in each partition (sending 100
packets). First one machine send 100 packets and after another. In
total we have 200 packages being sended by each experiment.

#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both :tangle data/ping/create_csv.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755)
echo "from,to,time"

for f in *_ping_*; do

    NODES=$(cat $f | grep Origem |\
		sed -E "s/.*: ([a-z]+[0-9]).*: ([a-z]+[0-9])/\1\n\2/g")

    ALMOST=$(cat $f | grep -A100 PING |\
		 sed -E "s/.*( [a-z]+[0-9] ).*time=([0-9.]+).*/\1,\2/g" |\
		 sed "s/ //g" | grep ,)

    echo "$NODES" | while read name; do

	echo "$ALMOST" | grep -v $name |\
	    sed -E "s/^/$name,/g"
    done
 done

#+end_src


#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
load <- function(dir=".", regex=".csv$") {

  options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
  suppressMessages(library(fs))
  suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

  BASE <- dir
  tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = regex, recurse=TRUE)) |> print() |>
    mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
    unnest(DATA) |> select(-CSV)
}

df <- load("data/ping/") |>
  mutate(partition = gsub("[0-9]*", "", from)) |>
  mutate(time = time/2) # [23:03:00; 21.02.2026]: ping gets the time to the
                        # packet to come back... So the time to go is half of it

df

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
library(DoE.base)
library(tidyverse)

fator_partition = c("cei", "draco", "poti", "tupi")
fator_app = c("lulesh", "comd", "minivite")
fator_nodes = c(1, 2, 4)
fator_exp_size = c("p", "m", "g")

fac.design(nfactors=4,
           replications=1,
           repeat.only= FALSE ,
           randomize=TRUE,
           seed=17366,
           nlevels=c(length(fator_partition),
                     length(fator_nodes),
                     length(fator_app),
                     length(fator_exp_size)),
           factor.names=list(
             partition = fator_partition,
             nodes = fator_nodes,
             app = fator_app,
             exp_size = fator_exp_size
           )) |>
  as_tibble() |>
  mutate_at(vars(nodes), as.character) |>
  mutate_at(vars(nodes), as.numeric) |>
  mutate(omp=1) |>
  mutate(np=8) |>
  mutate(Blocks=".1") |>
  select(partition,nodes,np,app,exp_size,omp,Blocks) |>
  filter(np >= nodes) |>
  print() |>
  write_csv("base.csv", progress=FALSE)
#+end_src

#+begin_src shell :results output :tangle scripts/run-real.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :exports both
#!/bin/bash
set +euxo pipefail
date

PROJECT=${1:-}
if [[ -z $PROJECT ]]; then
    echo "Path for project file not informed."
    exit 1
fi

echo "[REAL] Initializing Environment and Compiling"
# Carrega o Guix (use o Profile se já o tiver configurado para ser mais rápido!)
eval $(guix time-machine -C channels.scm -- shell -m guix.scm --search-paths)

# 1. Compila todas as aplicações UMA VEZ com o MPI Real antes do loop
echo "Compiling LULESH..."
pushd ./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/Coral/Lulesh/
make clean
make MPI_INC="" MPICXX="mpicxx -DUSE_MPI=1" -j 20
popd

echo "Compiling miniVite..."
pushd ./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/miniVite
make clean
make CXX=mpicxx OPTFLAGS="-O3 -fopenmp -DPRINT_DIST_STATS -DDEBUG_PRINTF" -j 20
popd

echo "Compiling CoMD..."
pushd ./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/src-mpi
make clean
make CC=mpicc -j 20
popd


BASEDIR="logs/$(basename -- PROJECT .csv)-$(date +%d-%m-%y)"
mkdir -p $BASEDIR

echo "[REAL] Reading CSV and Submitting Jobs"

tail -n +2 "$PROJECT" | while IFS=, read -r PARTICAO NODOS NP APP TAMANHO OMP B; do

    # Extrai o nível
    NIVEL=$(echo "$B" | sed -E "s/.*([0-9]+)/\1/g")
    DIR="${BASEDIR}/REAL-${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-${NIVEL}"
    mkdir -p "$DIR"

    HOSTFILE="$DIR/hosts.txt"

    # CORREÇÃO: O srun vai espalhar 8 tarefas e cada uma vai escrever
    # onde está rodando. Isso cria um arquivo com exatamente 8 linhas!
    srun hostname | sort > $HOSTFILE

    # Seleciona o executável e parâmetros com base na app
    case "$APP" in
        "lulesh")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/Coral/Lulesh/lulesh2.0"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 40" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 60" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "minivite")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/miniVite/miniVite"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-n 50000" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-n 200000" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-n 300000" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "comd")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/bin/CoMD-mpi"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 10 -y 10 -z 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 30 -y 30 -z 30" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 50 -y 50 -z 50" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        ,*)
            echo "Unknown application: $APP. Skipping..."
            continue
            ;;
    esac

    # ========================================================
    # CRIAÇÃO DINÂMICA DO SCRIPT DO SLURM
    # ========================================================
    SLURM_SCRIPT="$DIR/job.slurm"

    # O comando 'cat <<EOF' gera um arquivo de texto preenchendo as variáveis instantaneamente
    cat <<EOF > "$SLURM_SCRIPT"
#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name=Real_${APP}_${NIVEL}
#SBATCH --partition=${PARTICAO}
#SBATCH --nodes=${NODOS}
#SBATCH --ntasks=${NP}
#SBATCH --cpus-per-task=${OMP}
#SBATCH --output=${DIR}/exec_real.out
#SBATCH --error=${DIR}/exec_real.err
#SBATCH --time=01:00:00

# Carrega o ambiente no nó de execução
eval \$(guix time-machine -C channels.scm -- shell -m guix.scm --search-paths)

export OMP_NUM_THREADS=${OMP}

echo "[REAL] Starting execution..."

# Medição de Energia Inicial (Distribuída por todos os nós alocados pelo Slurm)
srun --nodes=${NODOS} --ntasks=${NODOS} bash -c "hostname; cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj"  > "${DIR}/start_uj"

# O mpirun nativo lê a alocação do Slurm automaticamente (sem necessidade de hostfile)
mpirun -np $NP -hostfile $HOSTFILE ${EXEC_BIN} ${PARAMETERS} > "${DIR}/$APP.out"

# Medição de Energia Final
srun --nodes=${NODOS} --ntasks=${NODOS} bash -c "hostname; cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj"  > "${DIR}/end_uj"

echo "[REAL] Execution finished."
EOF

    # Submete o script recém-criado para a fila do Slurm!
    sbatch "$SLURM_SCRIPT"
    echo "Submetido: $APP ($NODOS nós) -> Partição $PARTICAO"

    # Pausa de meio segundo para não sobrecarregar o Slurm Controller
    sleep 0.5

done
#+end_src

#+begin_src shell :results output :tangle scripts/run-sim.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :exports both
#!/bin/bash

set +euxo pipefail
date

PROJECT=${1:-}
if [[ -z $PROJECT ]]; then
    echo "Path for project file not informed."
fi

eval $(guix time-machine -C channels.scm -- shell -m guix.scm --search-paths)

make clean
make pcad

BASEDIR="logs/$(basename -- PROJECT .csv)-$(date +%d-%m-%y)"
mkdir -p $BASEDIR

tail -n +2 "$PROJECT" | while IFS=, read -r PARTICAO NODOS NP APP TAMANHO OMP B; do

    echo "[SMPI] Initializaion of simulation"

    DIR="${BASEDIR}/${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-$(echo "$B" | sed -E "s/.*([0-9]+)/\1/g")"
    mkdir -p $DIR

    echo "[SMPI] $APP with $NODOS ($NP process) in $PARTICAO"

    HOSTFILE="$DIR/hostfile.txt"
    rm -f "$HOSTFILE"

    RANKS_PER_NODE=$(( NP / NODOS ))
    REMAINDER=$(( NP % NODOS ))

    for ((i=1; i<=NODOS; i++)); do
        RANKS=$RANKS_PER_NODE
        if (( i <= REMAINDER )); then
	    RANKS=$((RANKS + 1))
        fi

        for ((j=1; j<=RANKS; j++)); do
	    echo "${PARTICAO}${i}" >> "$HOSTFILE"
        done
    done

    case "$APP" in
	"lulesh")

	    APP_DIR="./SMPI-proxy-apps/Benchmarks/Coral/Lulesh/"
	    pushd $APP_DIR
	    {
		make clean
		make MPI_INC="" MPICXX="smpicxx -DUSE_MPI=1" -j 20
	    }
	    popd

	    APP="${APP_DIR}/lulesh2.0 -i 100"

	    case $TAMANHO in
		"p") PARAMETERS="-s 10" ;;
		"m") PARAMETERS="-s 40" ;;
		"g") PARAMETERS="-s 60" ;;
	    esac
	    ;;

	"minivite")

	    APP_DIR="./SMPI-proxy-apps/Benchmarks/ECP/miniVite"
	    pushd $APP_DIR
	    {
		make clean
		make CXX=smpicxx OPTFLAGS="-O3 -fopenmp -DPRINT_DIST_STATS -DDEBUG_PRINTF" -j 20
	    }
	    popd

	    APP="${APP_DIR}/miniVite"
	    case $TAMANHO in
		"p") PARAMETERS="-n 50000" ;;
		"m") PARAMETERS="-n 200000" ;;
		"g") PARAMETERS="-n 300000" ;;
	    esac
	    ;;

	"comd")

	    APP_DIR="./SMPI-proxy-apps/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD"
	    pushd $APP_DIR/src-mpi
	    {
		make clean
		make CC=smpicc -j 20
	    }
	    popd

	    APP="${APP_DIR}/bin/CoMD-mpi -N 100"
	    case $TAMANHO in
		"p") PARAMETERS="-x 10 -y 10 -z 10" ;;
		"m") PARAMETERS="-x 30 -y 30 -z 30" ;;
		"g") PARAMETERS="-x 50 -y 50 -z 50" ;;
	    esac
	    ;;

	,*)
	    echo "Unknow application. Exiting..."
	    exit
	    ;;
    esac


    export OMP_NUM_THREADS=$OMP
    echo "[SMPI] Starting simulation..."
    cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj > "$DIR/start_uj"

    # Cei speed as I will run all in cei.
    smpirun -np $NP -hostfile $HOSTFILE -platform ./pcad.so --cfg=smpi/host-speed:19.125Gf $APP $PARAMETERS > "$DIR/smpi-$APP.out"

    cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj > "$DIR/end_uj"
done

date
#+end_src

[22:57:37; 23.02.2026]: To compile:

# MiniVite:
make CXX=smpicxx OPTFLAGS="-O3 -fopenmp -DPRINT_DIST_STATS -DDEBUG_PRINTF" -j $NUMBER_OF_PROCESSORS

# CoMD
make CC=smpicc -j $NUMBER_OF_PROCESSORS

baseando na execução sequencial das aplicações...
| Application    | rapido ~1s         | medio ~[2, 10]s    | demorado ~[20-60]s  |
|----------------+--------------------+--------------------+---------------------|
| Lulesh (i,s)   | i=100,s=10 -> 0.20 | i=100,s=30 -> 4.40 | i=100,s=75 -> 56.16 |
| MiniVite (n)   | n=50000 -> 0.63s   | n=180000 -> ~2     | n=180000 -> ~30     |
| CoMD (x=y=z,N) | x=10, N=100        | x=25, N=100        | x=50, n=100         |

[00:42:40; 24.02.2026]: I reduced the project because I fear that the
time taken to run everything will be really high...

*** 2026-02-24
Parsing the results:

#+begin_src shell :results output :tangle data/validation/parse.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :exports both

BASE=${1:-}

if [[ "$BASE" == "" ]]; then
    BASE="."
fi

echo "partition,nodes,np,app,size,omp,run,time,start_uj,end_uj";

for i in `find $BASE -name *lulesh* -type d`; do

    config=$(echo $i | rev | cut -d/ -f1 | rev | sed s/-/,/g | sed s/REAL,//g)

    empty=$(find $i -name "*_uj" | wc -l)

    if [[ "$empty" == "2" ]]; then

	time=$(cat $i/*.out | grep "Elapsed time" | sed -E "s/.* ([0-9]+.[0-9]+) .*/\1/g")

	start_uj=$(cat $i/start_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')
	end_uj=$(cat $i/end_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')

	echo $config,$time,$start_uj,$end_uj

    fi


done


for i in `find $BASE -name *minivite* -type d`; do
    config=$(echo $i | rev | cut -d/ -f1 | rev | sed s/-/,/g | sed s/REAL,//g)

    empty=$(find $i -name "*_uj" | wc -l)

    if [[ "$empty" == "2" ]]; then

    time=$(cat $i/*.out | grep "Average total time" | sed -E "s/.* ([0-9]+.[0-9]+),.*/\1/g" | xargs)

    start_uj=$(cat $i/start_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')
    end_uj=$(cat $i/end_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')

    echo $config,$time,$start_uj,$end_uj

    fi

done

for i in `find $BASE -name *comd* -type d`; do
    config=$(echo $i | rev | cut -d/ -f1 | rev | sed s/-/,/g  | sed s/REAL,//g)

    empty=$(find $i -name "*_uj" | wc -l)

    if [[ "$empty" == "2" ]]; then

    time=$(cat $i/*.out | grep "^total" | tail -n 1 | awk '{print $6}')

    start_uj=$(cat $i/start_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')
    end_uj=$(cat $i/end_uj | grep -Ev "^[a-z]+" | awk '{s+=$1} END {print s}')

    echo $config,$time,$start_uj,$end_uj

    fi
done


#+end_src

[12:45:07; 24.02.2026]: Half of minivite was not execute due to error
in the parameters, looks like there is a restriction for the number of
process to be equal to an app parameter...

[13:19:27; 24.02.2026]: minivite didnt worked with OMP_NUM_THREADS=10,
good to know then.

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both

options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(fs))
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

BASE <- "."
tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = ".csv$", recurse=TRUE)) |>
  filter(!grepl("/", CSV)) |>
  print() |>
  mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
  separate(CSV, into=paste0("XX", 1:2), sep="_") |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  select(where=XX1, everything()) |>
  select(-XX2) -> df

df
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df |> group_by(where, partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  filter(!is.na(time)) |>
  mutate(start_uj=ifelse(start_uj < 0, end_uj, start_uj)) |>
  mutate(end_uj=ifelse(end_uj < 0, start_uj, end_uj)) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_time = mean(time),
    sd = sd(time),
    cv_time = sd/mean_time,
    mean_uj = mean(end_uj - start_uj),
    sd_uj = sd(end_uj - start_uj),
    cv_uj = sd_uj/mean_uj,
  ) |>
  arrange(-sd) |>
  print(n=150) -> df.stats
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both

meu_estilo <- function(base=20) {
    list(
        theme_bw(base_size = base),
        theme(
            legend.title = element_blank(),
            plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
            legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
            legend.position = "right",
            legend.justification = "left",
            legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
            legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
            axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
        ))
}
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df.stats |>
  filter(omp==1) |>
  group_by(partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  summarise(
    N=sum(N),
    mean_time_real = mean_time[where=="real"],
    mean_time_sim = mean_time[where=="sim"],
    mean_diff = abs(mean_time[where=="real"] - mean_time[where=="sim"]),
    cv_erro = mean_diff / mean_time[where=="real"] * 100
  ) |>
  arrange(-cv_erro) |>
  print(n=120)

#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports both :width 1000 :height 800 :session *R*
appl="minivite"
part="cei"
s="m"

df.jitter <- df |> filter(
                     ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np == 8
                   )

df.stats |> filter(
        ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np==8) |>
  ggplot(aes(y=mean_time, x= as.factor(nodes), fill=where, color=where)) +

    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_time - sd, ymax = mean_time + sd),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

  geom_point(size=7, alpha=0.8) +

 geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes), y = time, color=where),
    # Set the transparency (alpha) to 0.3 for a faint look
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 3
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ partition) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#5555ff", "sim" = "#ff5555")) +
  meu_estilo(30) +

  labs(
    title="",
  x="Nodes",
  y="Mean Time (s)"
  )
#+end_src

[19:50:42; 25.02.2026]: How to run the notebook on pcad

On pcad:
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both

poetry run jupyter  notebook --no-browser --ip=0.0.0.0 --port=8888
#+end_src

At my machine:
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
ssh -L 8888:cei1:8888 rrdmatos@pcad
#+end_src

Don't forget then tmux or screen

[13:02:34; 27.02.2026]: Dealing with a deadlock when running........

#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
#!/bin/bash
set +euxo pipefail
date

PROJECT=${1:-}
if [[ -z $PROJECT ]]; then
    echo "Path for project file not informed."
    exit 1
fi

mkdir -p $BASEDIR

    # Extrai o nível
    NIVEL=$(echo "$B" | sed -E "s/.*([0-9]+)/\1/g")
    DIR="${BASEDIR}/REAL-${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-${NIVEL}"
    mkdir -p "$DIR"


    # Seleciona o executável e parâmetros com base na app
    case "$APP" in
        "lulesh")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/Coral/Lulesh/lulesh2.0"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 40" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 60" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "minivite")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/miniVite/miniVite"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-n 50000 -l" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-n 200000 -l" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-n 300000 -l" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "comd")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/bin/CoMD-mpi"
            if [[ $NP == "8" ]]; then
	    	EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/bin/CoMD-mpi -i 2 -j 2 -k 2"
	    fi

            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 10 -y 10 -z 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 30 -y 30 -z 30" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 50 -y 50 -z 50" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        *)
            echo "Unknown application: $APP. Skipping..."
            continue
            ;;
    esac


    HOSTFILE="$DIR/hosts.txt"
    SLURM_SCRIPT="$DIR/job.slurm"


    cat <<EOF > "$SLURM_SCRIPT"
#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name=REAL-${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-${NIVEL}
#SBATCH --partition=${PARTICAO}
#SBATCH --nodes=${NODOS}
#SBATCH --ntasks=${NP}
#SBATCH --output=${DIR}/exec_real.out
#SBATCH --error=${DIR}/exec_real.err
#SBATCH --time=5:00

export GUIX_PROFILE="\$HOME/.guix-profiles/simgrid-env"
source "\$GUIX_PROFILE/etc/profile"

which mpirun

export OMP_NUM_THREADS=$OMP
export OMPI_MCA_btl_tcp_if_exclude="lo,docker0,143.54.0.0/16"
export OMPI_MCA_oob_tcp_if_exclude="lo,docker0,143.54.0.0/16"

#!/bin/bash
set +euxo pipefail
date

PROJECT=${1:-}
if [[ -z $PROJECT ]]; then
    echo "Path for project file not informed."
    exit 1
fi

BASEDIR="logs/REAL-$(basename -- $PROJECT .csv)-$(date +%d-%m-%y-%s)"
mkdir -p $BASEDIR

echo "========= [REAL] Reading CSV and Submitting Jobs ============"

tail -n +2 "$PROJECT" | while IFS=, read -r PARTICAO NODOS NP APP TAMANHO OMP B; do

    # Extrai o nível
    NIVEL=$(echo "$B" | sed -E "s/.*([0-9]+)/\1/g")
    DIR="${BASEDIR}/REAL-${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-${NIVEL}"
    mkdir -p "$DIR"


    # Seleciona o executável e parâmetros com base na app
    case "$APP" in
        "lulesh")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/Coral/Lulesh/lulesh2.0"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 40" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-i 100 -s 60" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "minivite")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/miniVite/miniVite"
            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-n 50000 -l" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-n 200000 -l" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-n 300000 -l" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        "comd")
            EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/bin/CoMD-mpi"
            if [[ $NP == "8" ]]; then
	    	EXEC_BIN="./SMPI-proxy-apps-real/Benchmarks/ECP/CoMD/bin/CoMD-mpi -i 2 -j 2 -k 2"
	    fi

            case $TAMANHO in
                "p") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 10 -y 10 -z 10" ;;
                "m") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 30 -y 30 -z 30" ;;
                "g") PARAMETERS="-N 100 -x 50 -y 50 -z 50" ;;
            esac
            ;;

        *)
            echo "Unknown application: $APP. Skipping..."
            continue
            ;;
    esac


    HOSTFILE="$DIR/hosts.txt"
    SLURM_SCRIPT="$DIR/job.slurm"


    cat <<EOF > "$SLURM_SCRIPT"
#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name=REAL-${PARTICAO}-${NODOS}-${NP}-${APP}-${TAMANHO}-${OMP}-${NIVEL}
#SBATCH --partition=${PARTICAO}
#SBATCH --nodes=${NODOS}
#SBATCH --ntasks=${NP}
#SBATCH --output=${DIR}/exec_real.out
#SBATCH --error=${DIR}/exec_real.err
#SBATCH --time=15:00

set +euxo pipefail

echo "[REAL] Carregando ambiente Guix..."
export GUIX_PROFILE="\$HOME/.guix-profiles/simgrid-env"
source "\$GUIX_PROFILE/etc/profile"

which mpirun

export OMP_NUM_THREADS=$OMP
#export OMPI_MCA_btl_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"
#export OMPI_MCA_oob_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"

export OMPI_MCA_btl_base_verbose=100
# TCP-specific verbosity (to see IP binding and connection attempts)
export OMPI_MCA_btl_tcp_verbose=100
# Out-of-band communication verbosity (the initial wire-up phase)
export OMPI_MCA_oob_base_verbose=100
# (Optional) See which network interfaces it actually detects
export OMPI_MCA_if_base_verbose=100

# 2. PLANO DE DADOS (Comunicação do OpenMPI entre os nós)

#export OMPI_MCA_btl_base_warn_component_unused=0

# Isso impede que os daemons de inicialização caiam no buraco negro do switch do draco/cei
#export PRTE_MCA_oob_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24,127.0.0.0/8"
#export ORTE_MCA_oob_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24,127.0.0.0/8"
#export PMIX_MCA_ptl_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24,127.0.0.0/8"

export OMPI_MCA_btl="tcp,self"
export OMPI_MCA_btl_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"
export OMPI_MCA_oob_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"

# ======================================================================
# 2. PLANO DE CONTROLE (Trava o mpirun/PRTE para não usar o IP 143.54.x.x)
# ======================================================================
export PRTE_MCA_oob_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"
export PRTE_MCA_ptl_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"
export PMIX_MCA_ptl_tcp_if_include="192.168.30.0/24"

# ======================================================================
# 3. ANTI-TIMEOUT (Desliga a varredura por IPv6)
# ======================================================================
export OMPI_MCA_oob_tcp_disable_ipv6=1
export OMPI_MCA_btl_tcp_disable_ipv6=1
export PRTE_MCA_oob_tcp_disable_ipv6=1

echo "[REAL] Energia inicial..."
srun --nodes=${NODOS} --ntasks=${NODOS} bash -c "hostname; cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj" > "${DIR}/start_uj"

echo "[REAL] Criando Host..."
srun hostname | sort > $HOSTFILE

echo "[REAL] Launching mpirun..."
mpirun -np ${NP} --hostfile $HOSTFILE \
    ${EXEC_BIN} ${PARAMETERS} > "${DIR}/${APP}.out"

srun --nodes=${NODOS} --ntasks=${NODOS} bash -c "hostname; cat /sys/class/powercap/intel-rapl/intel-rapl\:*/energy_uj" > "${DIR}/end_uj"

echo "[REAL] Execution finished."
EOF

    sbatch "$SLURM_SCRIPT"
    echo "Submetido: $APP ($NODOS nós) -> Partição $PARTICAO"

    sleep 0.2

done

echo "========= Todos os jobs foram enfileirados! Use 'squeue -u \$USER' para acompanhar. ============"

options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(fs))
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

BASE <- "."
tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = ".csv$", recurse=TRUE)) |>
  filter(!grepl("/", CSV)) |>
  print() |>
  mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
  separate(CSV, into=paste0("XX", 1:2), sep="_") |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  select(where=XX1, everything()) |>
  select(-XX2) -> df

**** Statistics
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df |> group_by(where, partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  filter(!is.na(time)) |>
  mutate(start_uj=ifelse(start_uj < 0, end_uj, start_uj)) |>
  mutate(end_uj=ifelse(end_uj < 0, start_uj, end_uj)) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_time = mean(time),
    sd = sd(time),
    cv_time = sd/mean_time,
    mean_uj = mean(end_uj - start_uj),
    sd_uj = sd(end_uj - start_uj),
    cv_uj = sd_uj/mean_uj,
  ) |>
  arrange(-sd) |>
  print(n=150) -> df.stats

#+end_src

**** Graph style
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
meu_estilo <- function(base=20) {
    list(
        theme_bw(base_size = base),
        theme(
            legend.title = element_blank(),
            plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
            legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
            legend.position = "right",
            legend.justification = "left",
            legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
            legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
            axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
        ))
}
#+end_src

**** Graph


#+begin_src R :results graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports results :width 1000 :height 600 :session *R*
appl="lulesh"
part="cei"
s="g"


df.stats |> filter(
        ## partition==part &
                   app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np==8) |>
  ggplot(aes(y=mean_time, x= as.factor(nodes), fill=where, color=where)) +

    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_time - sd, ymax = mean_time + sd),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

  geom_point(size=4, alpha=0.8) +

 geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes), y = time, color=where),
    # Set the transparency (alpha) to 0.3 for a faint look
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 1
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ partition) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#5555ff", "sim" = "#ff5555")) +
  labs(
    x="Nodes",
    y="Mean Time (s)"
  ) +
  meu_estilo(25)

#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports results :width 1000 :height 600 :session *R*


df.jitter <- df |> filter(
                     ## partition==part &
                   app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np == 8
                   ) |>
  filter(end_uj - start_uj > 0)

df.stats |>
  mutate(mean_uj = ifelse(mean_uj < 0, 0, mean_uj)) |>
  filter(mean_uj > 0) |>
  filter(omp==1 & np==8 & size==s) |>

  ggplot(aes(x=as.factor(nodes), y=mean_uj, color=where)) +

  geom_point(size=4, alpha=0.8) +


    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_uj/1e6 - sd_uj/1e6, ymax = mean_uj/1e6 + sd_uj/1e6),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

   geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes),
        y = end_uj-start_uj,
        color=where),
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 1
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ partition) +
  labs(
    x="Nodes",
    y="Energy Consumption (J)"
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#ff9922", "sim" = "#497543")) +
  meu_estilo(25)

**** Continuing:
Get lines with negative values:

#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
cat data/validation/real_results.csv |\
    while read line; do

	# echo $line
	value=`echo $line | rev | cut -d, -f2,1 | rev | awk -F, '{print $2 - $1}'` # | sed -E "s/^(.*),(.*)$/\2 - \1/g" | tail -n +2`

	# echo $value
	if [[ $value -le 0 ]]; then
	    echo $line;
	fi;
    done
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both

options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(fs))
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

BASE <- "."
tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = ".csv$", recurse=TRUE)) |>
  filter(!grepl("/", CSV)) |>
  print() |>
  mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
  separate(CSV, into=paste0("XX", 1:2), sep="_") |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  select(where=XX1, everything()) |>
  select(-XX2) -> df

df
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df |> group_by(where, partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  filter(!is.na(time)) |>
  mutate(start_uj=ifelse(start_uj < 0, end_uj, start_uj)) |>
  mutate(end_uj=ifelse(end_uj < 0, start_uj, end_uj)) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_time = mean(time),
    sd = sd(time),
    cv_time = sd/mean_time,
    mean_uj = mean(end_uj - start_uj),
    sd_uj = sd(end_uj - start_uj),
    cv_uj = sd_uj/mean_uj,
  ) |>
  arrange(partition, nodes, app, size) |>
  print(n=150) -> df.stats
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
#+begin_example
`summarise()` has grouped output by 'where', 'partition', 'nodes', 'np', 'app', 'size'. You can override
using the `.groups` argument.

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both

meu_estilo <- function(base=20) {
    list(
        theme_bw(base_size = base),
        theme(
            legend.title = element_blank(),
            plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
            legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
            legend.position = "right",
            legend.justification = "left",
            legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
            legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
            axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
        ))
}
#+end_src

  filter(partition=="cei" &
         app=="lulesh") |>
  print(n=32)

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df.stats |>
  filter(omp==1) |>
  group_by(partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  summarise(
    N=sum(N),
    mean_time_real = mean_time[where=="real"],
    mean_time_sim = mean_time[where=="sim"],
    mean_diff = abs(mean_time[where=="real"] - mean_time[where=="sim"]),
    cv_erro = mean_diff / mean_time[where=="real"] * 100
  ) |>
  arrange(-cv_erro) |>
  print(n=120)

#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports both :width 1000 :height 800 :session *R*
appl="minivite"
part="cei"
s="m"

df.jitter <- df |> filter(
                     ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np == 8
                   )

df.stats |> filter(
        ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np==8) |>
  ggplot(aes(y=mean_time, x= as.factor(nodes), fill=where, color=where)) +

    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_time - sd, ymax = mean_time + sd),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

  geom_point(size=7, alpha=0.8) +

 geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes), y = time, color=where),
    # Set the transparency (alpha) to 0.3 for a faint look
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 3
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ partition) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#5555ff", "sim" = "#ff5555")) +
  meu_estilo(30) +

  labs(
    title="",
  x="Nodes",
  y="Mean Time (s)"
  )
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both

options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(fs))
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))

BASE <- "."
tibble(CSV = dir_ls(BASE, regexp = ".csv$", recurse=TRUE)) |>
  filter(!grepl("/", CSV)) |>
  print() |>
  mutate(DATA = map(CSV, read_csv, show_col_types=FALSE, progress=FALSE)) |>
  separate(CSV, into=paste0("XX", 1:2), sep="_") |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  select(where=XX1, everything()) |>
  select(-XX2) -> df

df
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
df |> group_by(where, partition, nodes, np, app, size, omp) |>
  filter(!is.na(time)) |>
  mutate(start_uj=ifelse(start_uj < 0, end_uj, start_uj)) |>
  mutate(end_uj=ifelse(end_uj < 0, start_uj, end_uj)) |>
  summarise(
    N=n(),
    mean_time = mean(time),
    sd = sd(time),
    cv_time = sd/mean_time,
    mean_uj = mean(end_uj - start_uj),
    sd_uj = sd(end_uj - start_uj),
    cv_uj = sd_uj/mean_uj,
  ) |>
  arrange(-sd) |>
  print(n=150) -> df.stats

#+end_src

**** Graph style
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both
meu_estilo <- function(base=20) {
    list(
        theme_bw(base_size = base),
        theme(
            legend.title = element_blank(),
            plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
            legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
            legend.position = "right",
            legend.justification = "left",
            legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
            legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
            axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
        ))
}
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports results :width 1000 :height 1000 :session *R*
appl="lulesh"
part="cei"
s="p"

df.jitter <- df |> filter(
                     ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
( where == "sim" |
 where == "basic2" |
 where == "local" |
 ## where == "shared" |
 where == "noMPI" |
 where == "real2") &
## size==s &
omp==1 &
np == 8
)


df.stats |> filter(
        ## partition==part &
                   ## app==appl &
( where == "sim" |
 where == "basic2" |
 where == "local" |
 ## where == "shared" |
 where == "noMPI" |
 where == "real2") &
## size==s &
omp==1 &
np==8) |>
  ggplot(aes(y=mean_time, x= as.factor(nodes), fill=where, color=where, shape=where)) +

    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_time - sd, ymax = mean_time + sd),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

  geom_point(size=4, alpha=0.7) +

 geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes), y = time, color=where),
    # Set the transparency (alpha) to 0.3 for a faint look
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 1
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ size ~ partition, scales="free") +
  ## scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#5555ff", "sim" = "#ff5555")) +
  labs(
    x="Nodes",
    y="Mean Time (s)"
  ) +
  meu_estilo(25)

#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output graphics file :file (org-babel-temp-file "figure" ".png") :exports results :width 1000 :height 600 :session *R*


df.jitter <- df |> filter(
                     ## partition==part &
                   app==appl &
                   size==s &
                   omp==1 &
                   np == 8
                   ) |>
  filter(end_uj - start_uj > 0)

df.stats |>
  mutate(mean_uj = ifelse(mean_uj < 0, 0, mean_uj)) |>
  filter(mean_uj > 0) |>
  filter(omp==1 & np==8 & size==s) |>

  ggplot(aes(x=as.factor(nodes), y=mean_uj, color=where)) +

  geom_point(size=4, alpha=0.8) +


    geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_uj/1e6 - sd_uj/1e6, ymax = mean_uj/1e6 + sd_uj/1e6),
    width = 0.2, # Controls the width of the horizontal bar at the end of the error line
    linewidth = 0.8, alpha = 1,
    color="black"
  ) +

   geom_jitter(
    data = df.jitter,
    aes(x = as.factor(nodes),
        y = end_uj-start_uj,
        color=where),
    alpha = 0.3,
    size = 1
  ) +
  facet_grid(app ~ partition) +
  labs(
    x="Nodes",
    y="Energy Consumption (J)"
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("real" = "#ff9922", "sim" = "#497543")) +
  meu_estilo(25)
#+end_src
